Starlight behavior for this configuration value is to use a trailing slash as many common hosting providers redirect to URLs with a trailing slash by default.

\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1285}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Minor Changes}{Minor Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1285}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2390}{\texttt{ \#2390}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/f493361d7b64a3279980e0f046c3a52196ab94e0}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily f493361}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Moves route data to {\ttfamily Astro.\+locals} instead of passing it down via component props

⚠️ {\bfseries{Breaking change\+:}} Previously, all of Starlight’s templating components, including user or plugin overrides, had access to a data object for the current route via {\ttfamily Astro.\+props}. This data is now available as {\ttfamily Astro.\+locals.\+starlight\+Route} instead.

To update, refactor any component overrides you have\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Remove imports of {\ttfamily @astrojs/starlight/props}, which is now deprecated.
\item Update code that accesses {\ttfamily Astro.\+props} to use {\ttfamily Astro.\+locals.\+starlight\+Route} instead.
\item Remove any spreading of {\ttfamily \{...Astro.\+props\}} into child components, which is no longer required.
\end{DoxyItemize}

In the following example, a custom override for Starlight’s {\ttfamily Last\+Updated} component is updated for the new style\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ Default\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight/components/LastUpdated.astro';}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ import\ type\ \{\ Props\ \}\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight/props';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ const\ \{\ lastUpdated\ \}\ =\ Astro.props;}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ const\ \{\ lastUpdated\ \}\ =\ Astro.locals.starlightRoute;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ updatedThisYear\ =\ lastUpdated?.getFullYear()\ ===\ new\ Date().getFullYear();}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{updatedThisYear\ \&\&\ (}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ <Default\ \{...Astro.props\}><slot\ /></Default>}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ <Default><slot\ /></Default>}
\DoxyCodeLine{)\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


{\itshape Community Starlight plugins may also need to be manually updated to work with Starlight 0.\+32. If you encounter any issues, please reach out to the plugin author to see if it is a known issue or if an updated version is being worked on.}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2578}{\texttt{ \#2578}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/f895f75b17f36c826cc871ba1826e5ae1dff44ca}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily f895f75}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Deprecates the Starlight plugin {\ttfamily setup} hook in favor of the new {\ttfamily config\+:setup} hook which provides the same functionality.

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE\+:}}

The Starlight plugin {\ttfamily setup} hook is now deprecated and will be removed in a future release. Please update your plugins to use the new {\ttfamily config\+:setup} hook instead.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ default\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ name:\ 'plugin-\/with-\/translations',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ hooks:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ 'setup'(\{\ config\ \})\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ 'config:setup'(\{\ config\ \})\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ Your\ plugin\ configuration\ setup\ code}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2578}{\texttt{ \#2578}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/f895f75b17f36c826cc871ba1826e5ae1dff44ca}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily f895f75}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Exposes the built-\/in localization system in the Starlight plugin {\ttfamily config\+:setup} hook.

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE\+:}}

This addition changes how Starlight plugins add or update translation strings used in Starlight’s localization APIs. Plugins previously using the \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/plugins/\#injecttranslations}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily inject\+Translations()}}} callback function from the plugin \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/plugins/\#configsetup}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily config\+:setup}}} hook should now use the same function available in the \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/plugins/\#i18nsetup}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily i18n\+:setup}}} hook.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ default\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ name:\ 'plugin-\/with-\/translations',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ hooks:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ 'config:setup'(\{\ injectTranslations\ \})\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ 'i18n:setup'(\{\ injectTranslations\ \})\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ injectTranslations(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ en:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 'myPlugin.doThing':\ 'Do\ the\ thing',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ fr:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 'myPlugin.doThing':\ 'Faire\ le\ truc',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2777}{\texttt{ \#2777}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/88f42145888f3a04f20898fcb700c1e65be48bb2}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 88f4214}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/hippotastic}{\texttt{ @hippotastic}}! -\/ Updates {\ttfamily astro-\/expressive-\/code} dependency to the latest version (0.\+40).

This includes an update to the latest Shiki version (1.\+26.\+1), providing access to all current Shiki themes and syntax highlighting languages, and adding the config options {\ttfamily shiki.\+engine}, {\ttfamily shiki.\+bundled\+Langs}, {\ttfamily shiki.\+lang\+Alias} and {\ttfamily remove\+Unused\+Themes}. It also adds new style variants to the optional collapsible sections plugin.

See the \href{https://expressive-code.com/releases/\#0400}{\texttt{ Expressive Code release notes}} for full details.

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2728}{\texttt{ \#2728}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/e1873834d4a4328084a9ac056a089ee5b8f13103}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily e187383}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Updates minimum Pagefind dependency to v1.\+3.\+0, sets new defaults for Pagefind’s ranking options, and adds support for manually configuring the ranking options

The new ranking option defaults have been evaluated against Starlight’s own docs to improve the quality of search results. See \href{https://pagefind.app/docs/ranking/}{\texttt{ “\+Customize Pagefind\textquotesingle{}s result ranking”}} for more details about how they work.

\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1305}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Minor Changes}{Minor Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1305}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2612}{\texttt{ \#2612}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/8d5a4e8000d9e3a4bb9ca8178767cf3d8bc48773}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 8d5a4e8}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Adds support for Astro v5, drops support for Astro v4.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1306}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Upgrade Astro and dependencies}{Upgrade Astro and dependencies}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1306}
⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE\+:}} Astro v4 is no longer supported. Make sure you \href{https://docs.astro.build/en/guides/upgrade-to/v5/}{\texttt{ update Astro}} and any other official integrations at the same time as updating Starlight\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{npx\ @astrojs/upgrade}

\end{DoxyCode}


{\itshape Community Starlight plugins and Astro integrations may also need to be manually updated to work with Astro v5. If you encounter any issues, please reach out to the plugin or integration author to see if it is a known issue or if an updated version is being worked on.}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1307}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Update your collections}{Update your collections}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1307}
⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE\+:}} Starlight\textquotesingle{}s internal \href{https://docs.astro.build/en/guides/content-collections/}{\texttt{ content collections}}, which organize, validate, and render your content, have been updated to use Astro\textquotesingle{}s new Content Layer API and require configuration changes in your project.


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item {\bfseries{Move the content config file.}} This file no longer lives within the {\ttfamily src/content/config.\+ts} folder and should now exist at {\ttfamily src/content.\+config.\+ts}.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item {\bfseries{Edit the collection definition(s).}} To update the {\ttfamily docs} collection, a {\ttfamily loader} is now required\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ //\ src/content.config.ts}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ import\ \{\ defineCollection\ \}\ from\ "{}astro:content"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{+import\ \{\ docsLoader\ \}\ from\ "{}@astrojs/starlight/loaders"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ import\ \{\ docsSchema\ \}\ from\ "{}@astrojs/starlight/schema"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ export\ const\ collections\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ docs:\ defineCollection(\{\ schema:\ docsSchema()\ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ docs:\ defineCollection(\{\ loader:\ docsLoader(),\ schema:\ docsSchema()\ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \};}

\end{DoxyCode}


If you are using the \href{https://starlight.astro.build/guides/i18n/\#translate-starlights-ui}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily i18n} collection}} to provide translations for additional languages you support or override our default labels, you will need to update the collection definition in a similar way and remove the collection {\ttfamily type} which is no longer available\+:

\`{}\`{}\`{}diff // src/content.\+config.\+ts import \{ define\+Collection \} from "{}astro\+:content"{}; +import \{ docs\+Loader, i18n\+Loader \} from "{}@astrojs/starlight/loaders"{}; import \{ docs\+Schema, i18n\+Schema \} from "{}@astrojs/starlight/schema"{};

export const collections = \{
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item docs\+: define\+Collection(\{ schema\+: docs\+Schema() \}),
\item docs\+: define\+Collection(\{ loader\+: docs\+Loader(), schema\+: docs\+Schema() \}),
\item i18n\+: define\+Collection(\{ type\+: \textquotesingle{}data\textquotesingle{}, schema\+: i18n\+Schema() \}),
\item i18n\+: define\+Collection(\{ loader\+: i18n\+Loader(), schema\+: i18n\+Schema() \}), \}; \`{}\`{}\`{}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item {\bfseries{Update other collections.}} To update any other collections you may have, follow the \href{https://docs.astro.build/en/guides/upgrade-to/v5/\#updating-existing-collections}{\texttt{ “\+Updating existing collections”}} section in the Astro 5 upgrade guide.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

If you are unable to make any changes to your collections at this time, including Starlight\textquotesingle{}s default {\ttfamily docs} and {\ttfamily i18n} collections, you can enable the \href{https://docs.astro.build/en/reference/legacy-flags/}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily legacy.\+collections} flag}} to upgrade to v5 without updating your collections. This legacy flag exists to provide temporary backwards compatibility, and will allow you to keep your collections in their current state until the legacy flag is no longer supported.\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1308}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Patch Changes}{Patch Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1308}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1923}{\texttt{ \#1923}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/5269aad928773ae08b35ba8e19c0f2832d0d2c89}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 5269aad}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Overhauls the built-\/in localization system which is now powered by the \href{https://www.i18next.com/}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily i18next}}} library and available to use anywhere in your documentation website.

See the \href{https://starlight.astro.build/guides/i18n/\#using-ui-translations}{\texttt{ “\+Using UI translations”}} guide to learn more about how to access built-\/in UI labels or your own custom strings in your project. Plugin authors can also use the new \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/plugins/\#injecttranslations}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily inject\+Translations()}}} helper to add or update translation strings.

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE\+:}} The {\ttfamily Astro.\+props.\+labels} props has been removed from the props passed down to custom component overrides.

If you are relying on {\ttfamily Astro.\+props.\+labels} (for example to read a built-\/in UI label), you will need to update your code to use the new \href{https://starlight.astro.build/guides/i18n/\#using-ui-translations}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Astro.\+locals.\+t()}}} helper instead.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ \{\ Props\ \}\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight/props';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ The\ \`{}search.label`\ UI\ label\ for\ this\ page’s\ language:}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ searchLabel\ =\ Astro.locals.t('search.label');}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1255}{\texttt{ \#1255}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/6f3202b3eb747de8a1cfcba001ab618d5fdee44a}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 6f3202b}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/Fryuni}{\texttt{ @\+Fryuni}}! -\/ Adds support for server-\/rendered Starlight pages.

When building a project with {\ttfamily hybrid} or {\ttfamily server} output mode, a new {\ttfamily prerender} option on Starlight config can be set to {\ttfamily false} to make all Starlight pages be rendered on-\/demand\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ output:\ 'server',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ integrations:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ starlight(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ prerender:\ false,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1784}{\texttt{ \#1784}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/68f56a7ffd314b760443a057db9ed1a982dbe191}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 68f56a7}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Changes the hero component action button default \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/frontmatter/\#heroconfig}{\texttt{ variant}} from {\ttfamily minimal} to {\ttfamily primary}.

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE\+:}} If you want to preserve the previous appearance, hero component action buttons previously declared without a {\ttfamily variant} will need to be updated to include the {\ttfamily variant} property with the value {\ttfamily minimal}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{hero:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ actions:}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ link:\ https://github.com/astronaut/my-\/project}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ icon:\ external}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2168}{\texttt{ \#2168}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/e044feeae9a336a87db526107e5772b54ddc567f}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily e044fee}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ ⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE\+:}} Updates the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Starlight\+Page /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component {\ttfamily sidebar} prop to accept an array of \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/configuration/\#sidebaritem}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Sidebar\+Item}}}s like the main Starlight {\ttfamily sidebar} configuration in {\ttfamily astro.\+config.\+mjs}.

This change simplifies the definition of sidebar items in the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Starlight\+Page /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component, allows for shared sidebar configuration between the global {\ttfamily sidebar} option and {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Starlight\+Page /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component, and also enables the usage of autogenerated sidebar groups with the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Starlight\+Page /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component. If you are using the {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Starlight\+Page /\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component with a custom {\ttfamily sidebar} configuration, you will need to update the {\ttfamily sidebar} prop to an array of \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/configuration/\#sidebaritem}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily Sidebar\+Item}}} objects.

For example, the following custom page with a custom {\ttfamily sidebar} configuration defines a “\+Resources” group with a “\+New” badge, a link to the “\+Showcase” page which is part of the {\ttfamily docs} content collection, and a link to the Starlight website\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ src/pages/custom-\/page/example.astro}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{<StarlightPage}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ frontmatter=\{\{\ title:\ 'My\ custom\ page'\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ sidebar=\{[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ type:\ 'group',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ label:\ 'Resources',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ badge:\ \{\ text:\ 'New'\ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ items:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{\ type:\ 'link',\ label:\ 'Showcase',\ href:\ '/showcase/'\ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ type:\ 'link',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ label:\ 'Starlight',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ href:\ 'https://starlight.astro.build/',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ]\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ <p>This\ is\ a\ custom\ page\ with\ a\ custom\ component.</p>}
\DoxyCodeLine{</StarlightPage>}

\end{DoxyCode}


This configuration will now need to be updated to the following\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ src/pages/custom-\/page/example.astro}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{<StarlightPage}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ frontmatter=\{\{\ title:\ 'My\ custom\ page'\ \}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ sidebar=\{[}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ label:\ 'Resources',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ badge:\ \{\ text:\ 'New'\ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ items:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 'showcase',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{\ label:\ 'Starlight',\ link:\ 'https://starlight.astro.build/'\ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ]\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ <p>This\ is\ a\ custom\ page\ with\ a\ custom\ component.</p>}
\DoxyCodeLine{</StarlightPage>}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2105}{\texttt{ \#2105}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/81f8a2c9580ec07dd17e2f596b9b1b50fae8237a}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 81f8a2c}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Fixes an edge case in custom pagination link processing

Custom link values for {\ttfamily prev}/{\ttfamily next} in page frontmatter are now always used as authored. Previously this was not the case in some edge cases such as for the first and final pages in the sidebar.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2119}{\texttt{ \#2119}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/464685a3ce33e7ccc8d1d7365935732c87ba95e9}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 464685a}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/evadecker}{\texttt{ @evadecker}}! -\/ Improves styling of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}hr\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}blockquote\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}, and {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}code\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} within asides

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2025}{\texttt{ \#2025}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/47f32c196c5d840a6a45799ddf123d17c77274b0}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 47f32c1}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Removes the {\ttfamily /} search shortcut for \href{https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/character-key-shortcuts.html}{\texttt{ accessibility reasons}}.

⚠️ {\bfseries{Potentially breaking change\+:}} The {\ttfamily search.\+shortcut\+Label} UI string has been removed. If you were using this string in your custom UI, you will need to update your code.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2064}{\texttt{ \#2064}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/c5b47cbe1242f0b29b9212db72fe26590ab57d88}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily c5b47cb}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/SnowDingo}{\texttt{ @\+Snow\+Dingo}}! -\/ Improves styling of Markdown tables to work better in different contexts, including against different background colours like when used in asides.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/2031}{\texttt{ \#2031}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/2bab648be9ddc6bfe05562650b773f5158a9ed42}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 2bab648}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Makes sidebar entry parsing stricter in Starlight config

{\bfseries{⚠️ Potentially breaking change\+:}} Previously Starlight would accept a sidebar entry that matched one of its expected shapes, even if it included additional properties. For example, including both {\ttfamily link} and {\ttfamily items} was considered valid, with {\ttfamily items} being ignored. Now, it is an error to include more than one of {\ttfamily link}, {\ttfamily items}, or {\ttfamily autogenerate} in a sidebar entry.

If you see errors after updating, look for sidebar entries in the Starlight configuration in {\ttfamily astro.\+config.\+mjs} that include too many keys and remove the one that was previously ignored.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1874}{\texttt{ \#1874}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/eeba06ea7df962e8f0520e145d28b8c17cd32c18}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily eeba06e}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/lorenzolewis}{\texttt{ @lorenzolewis}}! -\/ Adds a new syntax for specifying sidebar link items for internal links

You can now specify an internal page using only its slug, either as a string, or as an object with a {\ttfamily slug} property\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{starlight(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ title:\ 'Docs\ with\ easier\ sidebars',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ sidebar:\ ['getting-\/started',\ \{\ slug:\ 'guides/installation'\ \}],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}


Starlight will use the linked page’s frontmatter to configure the sidebar link.

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1841}{\texttt{ \#1841}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/ee0cd38a1fae31717fe820e779baeabe693cd67a}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily ee0cd38a}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Adds support for {\ttfamily Astro.\+current\+Locale} and Astro’s i18n routing.

⚠️ {\bfseries{Potentially breaking change\+:}} Starlight now configures Astro’s {\ttfamily i18n} option for you based on its {\ttfamily locales} config.

If you are currently using Astro’s {\ttfamily i18n} option as well as Starlight’s {\ttfamily locales} option, you will need to remove one of these. In general we recommend using Starlight’s {\ttfamily locales}, but if you have a more advanced configuration you may choose to keep Astro’s {\ttfamily i18n} config instead.

\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1382}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Minor Changes}{Minor Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1382}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1846}{\texttt{ \#1846}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/2de6703971908cfc0df2915ebf89a63e0141f954}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 2de67039}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Updates {\ttfamily @astrojs/mdx} to v3 and enables MDX optimization by default

⚠️ {\bfseries{Potentially breaking change\+:}} MDX optimization speeds up builds (Starlight’s docs are building \texorpdfstring{$\sim$}{\string~}40\% faster for example), but restricts some advanced MDX features. See full details in the \href{https://docs.astro.build/en/guides/integrations-guide/mdx/\#optimize}{\texttt{ MDX optimization documentation}}.

Most Starlight users should be unaffected, but if you are using MDX files outside of Starlight pages with the {\ttfamily components} prop, you may see issues. You can disable optimization by adding MDX manually to your {\ttfamily integrations} array in {\ttfamily astro.\+config.\+mjs}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ defineConfig\ \}\ from\ 'astro/config';}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ import\ mdx\ from\ '@astrojs/mdx';}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ starlight\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ https://astro.build/config}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ default\ defineConfig(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ integrations:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ starlight(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ title:\ 'My\ docs',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ mdx(),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/640}{\texttt{ \#640}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/7dc503ea7993123a4aeff453d08de41cac887353}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 7dc503ea}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Adds support for syncing multiple sets of tabs on the same page.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1620}{\texttt{ \#1620}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/ca0678ca556d739bda9648edc1b79c764fdea851}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily ca0678ca}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/emjio}{\texttt{ @emjio}}! -\/ Adds support for translating the site title

⚠️ {\bfseries{Potentially breaking change\+:}} The shape of the {\ttfamily title} field on Starlight’s internal config object has changed. This used to be a string, but is now an object.

If you are relying on {\ttfamily config.\+title} (for example in a custom {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Site\+Title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} or {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Head\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} component), you will need to update your code. We recommend using the new \href{https://starlight.astro.build/reference/overrides/\#sitetitle}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily site\+Title} prop}} available to component overrides\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ \{\ Props\ \}\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight/props';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ The\ site\ title\ for\ this\ page’s\ language:}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ \{\ siteTitle\ \}\ =\ Astro.props;}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1613}{\texttt{ \#1613}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/61493e55f1a80362af13f98d665018376e987439}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 61493e55}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Adds new {\ttfamily draft} frontmatter option to exclude a page from production builds.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/640}{\texttt{ \#640}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/7dc503ea7993123a4aeff453d08de41cac887353}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 7dc503ea}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Updates the default {\ttfamily line-\/height} from {\ttfamily 1.\+8} to {\ttfamily 1.\+75}. This change avoids having a line height with a fractional part which can cause scripts accessing dimensions involving the line height to get an inconsistent rounded value in various browsers.

If you want to preserve the previous {\ttfamily line-\/height}, you can add the following custom CSS to your site\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{:root\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/line-\/height:\ 1.8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1383}{\texttt{ \#1383}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/490c6eff34ab408c4f55777b7b0caa16787dd3d4}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 490c6ef}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Refactors Starlight’s internal virtual module system for components to avoid circular references

This is a change to an internal API. If you were importing the internal {\ttfamily virtual\+:starlight/components} module, this no longer exists. Update your imports to use the individual virtual modules now available for each component, for example {\ttfamily virtual\+:starlight/components/\+Edit\+Link}.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1151}{\texttt{ \#1151}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/134292ddd89683007d7de25545d39738a82c626c}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 134292d}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/kevinzunigacuellar}{\texttt{ @kevinzunigacuellar}}! -\/ Fixes sidebar auto-\/generation issue when a file and a directory, located at the same level, have identical names.

For example, {\ttfamily src/content/docs/guides.\+md} and {\ttfamily src/content/docs/guides/example.\+md} will now both be included and {\ttfamily src/content/docs/guides.\+md} is treated in the same way a {\ttfamily src/content/docs/guides/index.\+md} file would be.
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1386}{\texttt{ \#1386}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/0163634abb8578ce7a3d7ceea36432e98ea70e78}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 0163634}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Tightens {\ttfamily line-\/height} on {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}Link\+Card\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} titles to fix regression from original design

If you want to preserve the previous {\ttfamily line-\/height}, you can add the following custom CSS to your site\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{.sl-\/link-\/card\ a\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ line-\/height:\ 1.6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1376}{\texttt{ \#1376}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/8398432aa4a0f38e2dd4452dfcdf7033c5713334}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 8398432}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Tweaks vertical spacing in Markdown content styles.

This is a subtle change to Starlight’s default content styling that should improve most sites\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Default vertical spacing between content items is reduced from {\ttfamily 1.\+5rem} to {\ttfamily 1rem}.
\item Spacing before headings is now relative to font size, meaning higher-\/level headings have slightly more spacing and lower-\/level headings slightly less.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The overall impact is to tighten up content that belongs together and improve the visual hierarchy of headings to break up sections.

Although this is a subtle change, we recommend visually inspecting your site in case this impacts layout of any custom CSS or components.

If you want to preserve the previous spacing, you can add the following custom CSS to your site\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{/*\ Restore\ vertical\ spacing\ to\ match\ Starlight\ v0.15\ and\ below.\ */}
\DoxyCodeLine{.sl-\/markdown-\/content}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ :not(a,\ strong,\ em,\ del,\ span,\ input,\ code)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +\ :not(a,\ strong,\ em,\ del,\ span,\ input,\ code,\ :where(.not-\/content\ *))\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ margin-\/top:\ 1.5rem;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{.sl-\/markdown-\/content}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ :not(h1,\ h2,\ h3,\ h4,\ h5,\ h6)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +\ :is(h1,\ h2,\ h3,\ h4,\ h5,\ h6):not(:where(.not-\/content\ *))\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ margin-\/top:\ 2.5rem;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1372}{\texttt{ \#1372}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/773880de87b79bf3107dbc32df29a86dd11e4e6f}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 773880d}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Updates the table of contents highlighting styles to prevent UI shifts when scrolling through a page.

If you want to preserve the previous, buggy styling, you can add the following custom CSS to your site\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{starlight-\/toc\ a[aria-\/current='true'],}
\DoxyCodeLine{starlight-\/toc\ a[aria-\/current='true']:hover,}
\DoxyCodeLine{starlight-\/toc\ a[aria-\/current='true']:focus\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ font-\/weight:\ 600;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ color:\ var(-\/-\/sl-\/color-\/text-\/invert);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ background-\/color:\ var(-\/-\/sl-\/color-\/text-\/accent);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1238}{\texttt{ \#1238}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/02a808e4a0b9ac2383576e3495f6a766b663d773}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 02a808e}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Add support for Astro v4, drop support for Astro v3

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE}} Astro v3 is no longer supported. Make sure you \href{https://docs.astro.build/en/guides/upgrade-to/v4/}{\texttt{ update Astro}} and any other integrations at the same time as updating Starlight.

Use the new {\ttfamily @astrojs/upgrade} command to upgrade Astro and Starlight together\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{npx\ @astrojs/upgrade}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1242}{\texttt{ \#1242}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/d8fc9e15bd2ae4c945b5a3856a6ce3b5629e8b29}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily d8fc9e1}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Enables link prefetching on hover by default

Astro v4’s \href{https://docs.astro.build/en/guides/prefetch}{\texttt{ prefetch}} support is now enabled by default. If {\ttfamily prefetch} is not set in {\ttfamily astro.\+config.\+mjs}, Starlight will use `prefetch\+: \{ prefetch\+All\+: true, default\+Strategy\+: \textquotesingle{}hover' \}\`{} by default.

If you want to preserve previous behaviour, disable link prefetching in {\ttfamily astro.\+config.\+mjs}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ defineConfig\ \}\ from\ 'astro/config';}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ starlight\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ default\ defineConfig(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ //\ Disable\ link\ prefetching:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ prefetch:\ false,}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ integrations:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ starlight(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1447}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Minor Changes}{Minor Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1447}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/1023}{\texttt{ \#1023}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/a3b80f71037504f2b8d7f1a641924215091122bb}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily a3b80f7}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/kevinzunigacuellar}{\texttt{ @kevinzunigacuellar}}! -\/ Respect the {\ttfamily trailing\+Slash} and {\ttfamily build.\+format} Astro options when creating Starlight navigation links.

⚠️ {\bfseries{Potentially breaking change\+:}} This change will cause small changes in link formatting for most sites. These are unlikely to break anything, but if you care about link formatting, you may want to change some Astro settings.

If you want to preserve Starlight’s previous behavior, set `trailing\+Slash\+: \textquotesingle{}always'{\ttfamily in your}astro.\+config.\+mjs\`{}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ defineConfig\ \}\ from\ 'astro/config';}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ starlight\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ default\ defineConfig(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ trailingSlash:\ 'always',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ integrations:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ starlight(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ //\ ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/742}{\texttt{ \#742}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/c6a4bcb7982c54c513f20c96a9b2aaf9ac09094b}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily c6a4bcb}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/hippotastic}{\texttt{ @hippotastic}}! -\/ Adds Expressive Code as Starlight’s default code block renderer

⚠️ {\bfseries{Potentially breaking change\+:}} This addition changes how Markdown code blocks are rendered. By default, Starlight will now use \href{https://github.com/expressive-code/expressive-code/tree/main/packages/astro-expressive-code}{\texttt{ Expressive Code}}. If you were already customizing how code blocks are rendered and don\textquotesingle{}t want to use the \href{https://starlight.astro.build/guides/authoring-content/\#expressive-code-features}{\texttt{ features provided by Expressive Code}}, you can preserve the previous behavior by setting the new config option {\ttfamily expressive\+Code} to {\ttfamily false}.

If you had previously added Expressive Code manually to your Starlight project, you can now remove the manual set-\/up in {\ttfamily astro.\+config.\+mjs}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Move your configuration to Starlight’s new {\ttfamily expressive\+Code} option.
\item Remove the {\ttfamily astro-\/expressive-\/code} integration.
\end{DoxyItemize}

For example\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ starlight\ from\ '@astrojs/starlight';}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ defineConfig\ \}\ from\ 'astro/config';}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ import\ expressiveCode\ from\ 'astro-\/expressive-\/code';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ default\ defineConfig(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ integrations:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ expressiveCode(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \ \ themes:\ ['rose-\/pine'],}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ \ \ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ starlight(\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ title:\ 'My\ docs',}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ expressiveCode:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \ \ themes:\ ['rose-\/pine'],}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ \ \ \ \ \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\});}

\end{DoxyCode}


Note that the built-\/in Starlight version of Expressive Code sets some opinionated defaults that are different from the {\ttfamily astro-\/expressive-\/code} defaults. You may need to set some {\ttfamily style\+Overrides} if you wish to keep styles exactly the same.

⚠️ {\bfseries{Potentially breaking change\+:}} The {\ttfamily hero.\+image} schema is now slightly stricter than previously.

The {\ttfamily hero.\+image.\+html} property can no longer be used alongside the {\ttfamily hero.\+image.\+alt} or {\ttfamily hero.\+image.\+file} properties. Previously, {\ttfamily html} was ignored when used with {\ttfamily file} and {\ttfamily alt} was ignored when used with {\ttfamily html}. Now, those combinations will throw errors. If you encounter errors, remove the {\ttfamily image.\+hero} property that is not in use.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/774}{\texttt{ \#774}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/903a57942ceb99b68672c3fa54622b39cc5d76f8}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 903a579}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Support adding HTML attributes to sidebar links from config and frontmatter
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/796}{\texttt{ \#796}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/372ec96d31d0c1a9aa8bc1605de2b424bf9bd5af}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 372ec96}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Add the {\ttfamily @astrojs/sitemap} and {\ttfamily @astrojs/mdx} integrations only if they are not detected in the Astro configuration.

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE}} The minimum supported version of Astro is now v3.\+2.\+0. Make sure you update Astro at the same time as updating Starlight\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{npm\ install\ astro@latest}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/447}{\texttt{ \#447}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/b45719b581353f8d8f0ce0a9b5c89132e902377b}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily b45719b}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/andremralves}{\texttt{ @andremralves}}! -\/ Add {\ttfamily title\+Delimiter} configuration option and include site title in page {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} tags

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE}} — Previously, every page’s {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} only included its individual frontmatter title. Now, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} tags include the page title, a delimiter character ({\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} by default), and the site title. For example, in the Startlight docs, {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}Configuration Reference\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}/title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} is now {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}Configuration Reference \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} Starlight\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}/title\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}.

If you have a page where you need to override this new behaviour, set a custom title using the {\ttfamily head} frontmatter property\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{title:\ My\ Page}
\DoxyCodeLine{head:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/\ tag:\ title}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ content:\ Custom\ Title}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/709}{\texttt{ \#709}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/140e729a8bf12f805ae0b7e2b5ad959cf68d8e22}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 140e729}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Add support for overriding Starlight’s built-\/in components

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE}} — The page footer is now included on pages with {\ttfamily template\+: splash} in their frontmatter. Previously, this was not the case. If you are using {\ttfamily template\+: splash} and want to continue to hide footer elements, disable them in your frontmatter\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{title:\ Landing\ page}
\DoxyCodeLine{template:\ splash}
\DoxyCodeLine{\#\ Disable\ unwanted\ footer\ elements\ as\ needed}
\DoxyCodeLine{editUrl:\ false}
\DoxyCodeLine{lastUpdated:\ false}
\DoxyCodeLine{prev:\ false}
\DoxyCodeLine{next:\ false}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/-\/-\/}

\end{DoxyCode}


⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE}} — This change involved refactoring the structure of some of Starlight’s built-\/in components slightly. If you were previously overriding these using other techniques, you may need to adjust your code.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/529}{\texttt{ \#529}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/c2d0e7f2699e60a48a3a9074eee6439dee8624a1}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily c2d0e7f}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ For improved compatibility with Tailwind, some Starlight built-\/in class names are now prefixed with {\ttfamily "{}sl-\/"{}}.

While not likely, if you were relying on one of these internal class names in your own components or custom CSS, you will need to update to use the prefixed version.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{Before\+:}} {\ttfamily flex}, {\ttfamily md\+:flex}, {\ttfamily lg\+:flex}, {\ttfamily block}, {\ttfamily md\+:block}, {\ttfamily lg\+:block}, {\ttfamily hidden}, {\ttfamily md\+:hidden}, {\ttfamily lg\+:hidden}.
\item {\bfseries{After\+:}} {\ttfamily sl-\/flex}, {\ttfamily md\+:sl-\/flex}, {\ttfamily lg\+:sl-\/flex}, {\ttfamily sl-\/block}, {\ttfamily md\+:sl-\/block}, {\ttfamily lg\+:sl-\/block}, {\ttfamily sl-\/hidden}, {\ttfamily md\+:sl-\/hidden}, {\ttfamily lg\+:sl-\/hidden}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/470}{\texttt{ \#470}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/d076aec856921c2fe8a5204a0c31580a846af180}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily d076aec}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Drop support for the {\ttfamily -\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent} CSS custom property.

⚠️ {\bfseries{BREAKING CHANGE}} — In previous Starlight versions you could control the accent color by setting the {\ttfamily -\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent} custom property. This could result in inaccessible color contrast and unpredictable results.

You must now set accent colors directly. If you relied on setting {\ttfamily -\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent}, migrate by setting light and dark mode colors in your custom CSS\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{:root\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent:\ 234;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/color-\/accent-\/low:\ hsl(var(-\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent),\ 54\%,\ 20\%);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/color-\/accent:\ hsl(var(-\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent),\ 100\%,\ 60\%);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/color-\/accent-\/high:\ hsl(var(-\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent),\ 100\%,\ 87\%);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{:root[data-\/theme='light']\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/color-\/accent-\/high:\ hsl(var(-\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent),\ 80\%,\ 30\%);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/color-\/accent:\ hsl(var(-\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent),\ 90\%,\ 60\%);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/-\/sl-\/color-\/accent-\/low:\ hsl(var(-\/-\/sl-\/hue-\/accent),\ 88\%,\ 90\%);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The \href{https://starlight.astro.build/guides/css-and-tailwind/\#color-theme-editor}{\texttt{ new color theme editor}} might help if you’d prefer to set a new color scheme.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/237}{\texttt{ \#237}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/4279d7512a8261b576056471f5aa1ede1e6aae4a}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily 4279d75}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/HiDeoo}{\texttt{ @\+Hi\+Deoo}}! -\/ Use path instead of slugified path for auto-\/generated sidebar item configuration

⚠️ Potentially breaking change. If your docs directory names don’t match their URLs, for example they contain whitespace like {\ttfamily docs/my docs/}, and you were referencing these in an {\ttfamily autogenerate} sidebar group as {\ttfamily my-\/docs}, update your config to reference these with the directory name instead of the slugified version\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{autogenerate:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{-\/\ directory:\ 'my-\/docs',}
\DoxyCodeLine{+\ directory:\ 'my\ docs',}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1554}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Patch Changes}{Patch Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2_0dastrojs_2starlight_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md1554}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/pull/78}{\texttt{ \#78}} \href{https://github.com/withastro/starlight/commit/d3ee6fc643de7a320a6bb83432cdcfbb0a4e4289}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily d3ee6fc}}} Thanks \href{https://github.com/delucis}{\texttt{ @delucis}}! -\/ Add support for customising and translating Starlight’s UI.

Users can provide translations in JSON files in {\ttfamily src/content/i18n/} which is a data collection. For example, a {\ttfamily src/content/i18n/de.\+json} might translate the search UI\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}search.label"{}:\ "{}Suchen"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}search.shortcutLabel"{}:\ "{}(Drücke\ /\ zum\ Suchen)"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


This change also allows Starlight to provide built-\/in support for more languages than just English and adds German \& Spanish support.
